 The cabinet has approved the new aviation policy
 buudhvaar ko piem modi kii adhyakshata main hui baithak main yah faisla kiya gaya he
 Under the new policy, now a fare of Rs 2500 will have to be paid for 1 hour journey, while Rs 1200 will have to be paid for 30 minutes
 nai policy main yatriyon ke hiton kaa dhyaan rakhaa gaya he
 After the implementation of the new policy, now passengers will get refund within 15 days on cancellation of domestic tickets, while refund will be given within 30 days on cancellation of international tickets
 agar koi yatri apana tikat cancil karwaata he to cancellation charge ke taur par 200 rupye se zyada vasula nahin ja saktaa
 Now aviation companies will need 20 aircraft for international flights but will not have to wait for five years to start international service

 For good skin, there is hardly any other cheaper and better solution than turmeric
 ye ek aisa antiseptic he jise aap rojaanaa istemaal kar sakati hai
 It is very effective in cleansing the skin as well as improving it
 aamtaur par ham sabhi apane gharon main haldi kaa istemaal khaane kii rangath badhaane or swaad ke liye karte hai lekin ye ek acha beauty product bhi he
 There is hardly any beauty product better than this in a low budget
 haldi ko bataur beauty product kuch is tarah se istemaal kar sakate hai:1
 Mix a little water and sandalwood powder in turmeric powder and prepare a pack
 is pack ko kareeb 10 minute tak chehre par lagaakar rakhen
 Later clean it with cold water
 aise karne se keel-muhaanse saaf ho jaaenge
 2
 haldi ke powder main do-chaar buundasarson kaa telor kuch boonden neembu kii mila len
 Keep it on the face for a while
 jab ye sookhne lage to ise chehre par halke haathon se malkar utaar len
 It will work like a natural scrub
 3
 Prepare a thick paste by mixing turmeric powder, few drops of lemon and cucumber juice
 ise puure chehre or gale par lagaakar thodi der ke liye chhod den
 This will clear the dark spots
 4
 Turmeric powder is an effective remedy for wrinkle problems
 butter milk main haldi powder milakar chehre or gale par lagaaein
 Let it dry thoroughly
 baad main ise thande pani se dho len
 Doing so will benefit the Wrinkle problem
 5
 By applying butter-milk and turmeric paste on the body before bathing every day, dead skin is cleaned
 jisase twachaa komal bani rahati he
 6
 haldi or nariyal tel ko milakar ek paste taiyaar kar len
 Applying this paste on torn ankles provides relief
 7
 Grind turmeric with neem leaves
 is paste ko puure sharir par achche se mel len
 This will kill the bacteria present on the skin
